<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Other Events. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Redemption of 1.000% Notes Due 2022 </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;1, 2021, Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release calling for redemption the entire &#8364;500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 1.000% Notes due 2022 (CUSIP No.&#160;609207AD7 / ISIN No.&#160;XS1197269647) (the &#8220;1.000% Notes&#8221;), which were issued pursuant to the Indenture, dated as of March&#160;6, 2015 (as supplemented and amended from time to time, the &#8220; 2015 Base Indenture&#8221;), by and between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee, as supplemented by the Officers&#8217; Certificate of the Company, dated as of March&#160;6, 2015, issued pursuant to Section&#160;301 of the 2015 Base Indenture. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 1.000% Notes will be redeemed on March&#160;31, 2021 (the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;), at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 1.000% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&#160;the sum of the present values of the Remaining Scheduled Payments (as defined in the 1.000% Notes) discounted to the Redemption Date, on an annual basis (ACTUAL/Actual (ICMA)) (as defined in the 1.000% Notes) at rate equal to the applicable Treasury Rate (as defined in the 1.000% Notes) plus 15 basis points, plus, in either case, accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Redemption of 1.625% Notes Due 2023 </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;1, 2021, the Company issued a press release calling for redemption the entire &#8364;700,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 1.625% Notes due 2023 (CUSIP No.&#160;609207AJ4 / ISIN No.&#160;XS1346872580) (the &#8220;1.625% Notes&#8221;), which were issued pursuant to the 2015 Base Indenture, as supplemented by the Officers&#8217; Certificate of the Company, dated as of January&#160;21, 2016, issued pursuant to Section&#160;301 of the 2015 Base Indenture. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 1.625% Notes will be redeemed on the Redemption Date at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 1.625% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&#160;the sum of the present values of the Remaining Scheduled Payments (as defined in the 1.625% Notes) discounted to the Redemption Date, on an annual basis (ACTUAL/Actual (ICMA)) (as defined in the 1.625% Notes) at a rate equal to the applicable Treasury Rate (as defined in the 1.625% Notes) plus 25 basis points, plus, in either case, accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Redemption of 2.125% Notes Due 2023 </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;1, 2021, the Company issued a press release calling for redemption the entire $500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 2.125% Notes due 2023 (CUSIP No. 609207AS4 / ISIN No. US609207AS49) (the &#8220;2.125% Notes&#8221;), which were issued pursuant to the 2015 Base Indenture, as supplemented by the Officers&#8217; Certificate of the Company, dated as of April&#160;13, 2020, issued pursuant to Section&#160;301 of the 2015 Base Indenture. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2.125% Notes will be redeemed on the Redemption Date at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 2.125% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&#160;the sum of the present values of each remaining scheduled payment of principal and interest thereon (exclusive of interest accrued to the Redemption Date) that would have been payable if the 2.125% Notes matured on March&#160;13, 2023 discounted to the Redemption Date on a semi-annual basis (assuming a <span style="white-space:nowrap">360-day</span> year consisting of twelve <span style="white-space:nowrap">30-day</span> months) at the Treasury Rate (as defined in the 2.125% Notes) plus 30 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />


<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><span style="font-style:italic">Redemption of 4.000% Notes Due 2024 </span></p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On March&#160;1, 2021, the Company issued a press release calling for redemption of the $492,460,000 outstanding amount of the $1,750,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 4.000% Notes due 2024 (CUSIP No. 609207AB1 / ISIN No. US609207AB14) (the &#8220;4.000% Notes&#8221;), which were issued pursuant to the Indenture, dated as of October&#160;17, 2001 (as supplemented and amended from time to time, the &#8220;2001 Base Indenture&#8221;), by and between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas (as successor to The Bank of New York, as successor to The Chase Manhattan Bank), as trustee, as supplemented by the Officers&#8217; Certificate of the Company, dated as of January&#160;16, 2014, issued pursuant to Section&#160;301 of the 2001 Base Indenture. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 4.000% Notes will be redeemed on the Redemption Date at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 4.000% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&#160;the sum of the present values of each remaining scheduled payment of principal and interest thereon (exclusive of interest accrued to the Redemption Date) discounted to the Redemption Date on a semi-annual basis (assuming a <span style="white-space:nowrap">360-day</span> year consisting of twelve <span style="white-space:nowrap">30-day</span> months) at the Treasury Rate (as defined in the 4.000% Notes) plus 17.5 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest on the principal amount of the 4.000% Notes to, but not including, the Redemption Date. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company expects to publish the actual redemption prices for the 1.000% Notes, the 1.625% Notes, the 2.125% Notes and the 4.000% Notes in the investor section of its website (http://www.mondelezinternational.com/investors) once they have been determined. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Calls for </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Redemption of 1.000% Notes due 2022, </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>1.625% Notes Due 2023, 2.125% Notes due 2023 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>and 4.000% Notes due 2024 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CHICAGO, IL, March&nbsp;1, 2021 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) (&#147;Mondel&#275;z International&#148; or the
&#147;Company&#148;) today called for redemption the entire &#128;500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 1.000% Notes due 2022 (CUSIP&nbsp;No.&nbsp;609207AD7 / ISIN&nbsp;No.&nbsp;XS1197269647) (the &#147;1.000% Notes&#148;), the
entire &#128;700,000,000 aggregate principal amount of its outstanding 1.625% Notes due 2023 (CUSIP&nbsp;No.&nbsp;609207AJ4 / ISIN&nbsp;No.&nbsp;XS1346872580) (the &#147;1.625% Notes&#148;), and the entire $500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of
its outstanding 2.125% Notes due 2023 (CUSIP&nbsp;No.&nbsp;609207AS4 / ISIN&nbsp;No.&nbsp;US609207AS49) (the &#147;2.125% Notes&#148;), which were issued pursuant to the Indenture, dated as of March&nbsp;6, 2015 (as supplemented and amended from
time to time, the &#147;2015 Base Indenture&#148;), by and between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee, as supplemented by the Officers&#146; Certificate of the Company, dated as of March&nbsp;6, 2015, the Officers&#146;
Certificate of the Company, dated as of January&nbsp;21, 2016, and the Officers&#146; Certificate of the Company, dated as of April&nbsp;13, 2020, issued pursuant to Section&nbsp;301 of the 2015 Base Indenture. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company also called for redemption of the remaining $492,460,000 outstanding amount of the $1,750,000,000 aggregate principal amount of
its outstanding 4.000% Notes due 2024 (CUSIP No. 609207AB1 / ISIN No. US609207AB14) (the &#147;4.000% Notes&#148; and, together with the 1.000% Notes, the 1.625% Notes and the 2.125% Notes, the &#147;Notes&#148;), which were issued pursuant to the
Indenture, dated as of October&nbsp;17, 2001 (as supplemented and amended from time to time, the &#147;2001 Base Indenture&#148;), by and between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas (as successor to The Bank of New York, as
successor to The Chase Manhattan Bank), as trustee, as supplemented by the Officers&#146; Certificate of the Company, dated as of January&nbsp;16, 2014, issued pursuant to Section&nbsp;301 of the 2001 Base Indenture. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Notes will be redeemed on March&nbsp;31, 2021 (the &#147;Redemption Date&#148;). The
1.000% Notes will be redeemed at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 1.000% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&nbsp;the sum of the present values of the Remaining Scheduled Payments (as defined in the 1.000%
Notes) discounted to the Redemption Date, on an annual basis (ACTUAL/Actual (ICMA)) (as defined in the 1.000% Notes) at a rate equal to the applicable Treasury Rate (as defined in the 1.000% Notes) plus 15 basis points, plus, in either case, accrued
and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 1.625% Notes will be redeemed at a redemption price
equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 1.625% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&nbsp;the sum of the present values of the Remaining Scheduled Payments (as defined in the 1.625% Notes) discounted to the Redemption Date, on an
annual basis (ACTUAL/Actual (ICMA)) (as defined in the 1.625% Notes) at a rate equal to the applicable Treasury Rate (as defined in the 1.625% Notes) plus 25 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the
Redemption Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2.125% Notes will be redeemed at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the
2.125% Notes to be redeemed or (2)&nbsp;the sum of the present values of each remaining scheduled payment of principal and interest thereon (exclusive of interest accrued to the Redemption Date) that would have been payable if the 2.125% Notes
matured on March&nbsp;13, 2023 discounted to the Redemption Date on a semi-annual basis (assuming a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">360-day</FONT> year consisting of twelve <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> months) at the Treasury Rate
(as defined in the 2.125% Notes) plus 30 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest, if any, thereon to, but excluding, the Redemption Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 4.000% Notes will be redeemed at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the 4.000% Notes to be
redeemed or (2)&nbsp;the sum of the present values of each remaining scheduled payment of principal and interest thereon (exclusive of interest accrued to the Redemption Date) discounted to the Redemption Date on a semi-annual basis (assuming a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">360-day</FONT> year consisting of twelve <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> months) at the Treasury Rate (as defined in the 4.000% Notes) plus 17.5 basis points, plus accrued and unpaid interest on the
principal amount of the 4.000% Notes to, but not including, the Redemption Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company expects to publish the actual redemption
prices of the Notes in the investor section of its website (<U>http://www.mondelezinternational.com/investors</U>) once they have been determined. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2020 net revenues
of approximately $27&nbsp;billion, Mondel&#275;z International is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>OREO</I>, <I>belVita</I> and <I>LU</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury</I> <I>Dairy Milk</I>, <I>Milka</I> and
<I>Toblerone</I> chocolate; <I>Sour Patch Kids</I> candy and <I>Trident</I> gum. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This press

..report .reu td {
	border-bottom: 1px solid black;
}

	background-color: white;
}

	border-bottom: 1px solid black;
}

	border-bottom: 0px solid black;
}

	white-space: nowrap;
}

	text-align: right;
	white-space: nowrap;
}

	padding-left: 2em;
}

	padding: 0px 0.4em 0px 2em;
}

	text-align: left;
	white-space: normal;
}

	width: 17em;
}

}

}
